posted:Posted August 9, 2021
msg:This hotel was quiet, beautiful, delicious and half-empty. The receptionists don't speak English, but I think it's because the international market is closed now. But this does not exempt them from the obligation to acquaint a guest with the restaurant's working hours, shuttle bus services and other important points, which, unfortunately, they did not try to do and caused some doubts about their professionalism.¬† But Lady Shelley was very helpful and answered all questions, even late at night. It turned out that you can even get to the airport by shuttle bus, which I was happy to use. There is also a shuttle to the village and the entrance to Monkey Island. The hotel is located in a picturesque place, where there are very well-groomed trees and shrubs, there is a beautiful swimming pool decorated with tropical vegetation, and there are plenty of places where wedding shoots are held. The beach is mostly deserted, but there is a station for those who learn to surf, and the hotel provides discounts for its customers. People almost do not swim in the sea, and there are signs everywhere that it is forbidden to swim, the beach is beautiful, but it is not equipped for swimming. But you can find a few wooden sun beds, bring your own towel and lie there at least all day. The hotel does not provide a gym. There are very good paths for morning runs, and you can use the paths of the neighboring hotel, too. 
The breakfasts offer good food. It is almost the same every day, but the types of fish and meat changed, and everything was delicious. You can order lunch or dinner here in the restaurant, too. Right at the entrance to the hotel there are two supermarkets where you can buy food and drinks. The view of the sea from the room is quite limited, so there is no need to overpay for the sea view. Rather, it is a view of the pool and a little bit of the sea. The room has a large refrigerator, a kettle and even a microwave. So it is very suitable for a rest for 4-5 days.

The musty smell of the room and the smell of the bathroom are really bad. When you stay in the room, you have to open the balcony door. When you close it, the smell is great, above! There are spider webs in the corners on the drying rack on the balcony, there are dead bugs on the ground in the house, the wifi is not working well, the mobile phone signal in the house is not strong, the facilities are relatively old, the toilet flush button in the bathroom is very difficult to use , it is difficult to get out of the water, there is no small square towel to wipe hands, the lights in the house can only be pressed by the main switch at the door, and there is no bedside control switch, which is very inconvenient.
Besides the environment outside the hotel, the scope of activities is not large. There is a small children's activity area next to the lobby, a swimming pool outside, and a children's water park with a water depth of 0.2 meters. It is really only suitable for small children. The ordinary swimming pool is divided into deep water area and shallow water area. The deep water area is 1.5 meters and the shallow water area is 1.2 meters. The middle is separated by a float. I don‚Äôt know the deep water area, but I can‚Äôt feel 1.2 meters in the shallow water area. My child is 117 meters tall. , standing in the water to the chest, this depth is suitable for children to play, in comparison, children feel more secure in it, because they can step on the bottom of the pool with both feet! But I want to complain about the opening time of this swimming pool. I have stayed in many five-star hotels, but I have never encountered a swimming pool that is open at different times. The opening hours of this swimming pool are 9:30-12:30 and 16:00-21 :30, although it is very hot at noon, it does not mean that no one wants to swim. Maybe the hotel's consideration is that it is very hot at noon, so no one will swim, but this is only the hotel's consideration, not the choice of the guests. Think about it from the customer's point of view!
There are few types of breakfast, and there are not many choices. The standard is to be full, and the requirements cannot be too high!
Dinner is a la carte, not a buffet. The amount of dishes is poor. The vegetarian dishes are basically 58 servings, and the ordinary meat dishes are 88 servings. If you want to eat meat related to seafood, it is the 108 and 138 stalls. The price is second, but I I wonder if we can increase the amount of food a little bit more? A small fried Wenchang chicken, 88 yuan, is not served on a plate, but in a small casserole. The whole dish has five or six pieces of meat, and the rest are all onions. Your chicken is too expensive. Come on! To be honest, meat dishes are really not as good as vegetarian dishes. Although the amount is not large, there are no other side dishes to fill up, so compared to meat dishes, vegetarian dishes are more affordable. For more than 200 yuan, the family is not full, and it is absolutely amazing!
We can't order food at any time, and there are fixed points. The restaurant we arrived at 6 o'clock told us to start ordering food at 7 o'clock, and we could only sit on the seat and wait for an hour, and we couldn't reserve a seat. If you don't wait, If you come back at 7 o'clock, you are not sure if you can order it, and you may not be able to order until the next time slot! This is also weird! If you want me to say that because of the epidemic, everyone has no choice but to eat in the hotel restaurant. If not, can it be your turn to order meals for the guests? At this time, it should be more humane, and think more from the perspective of the guests!
The only thing that made me feel good during these three nights was the service at the front desk in the lobby. Especially at the beginning of the epidemic, the front desk actively answered the questions of the guests, helped the guests to follow up the development of the epidemic situation, and organized the guests to do nucleic acid tests. These are still very good. ! Also, the hotel's parking is very convenient. In addition to the parking space on the ground, there is also an underground parking lot, and the elevator is directly accessible, which is also the advantage of the hotel.
I really hope to change the details. Since it is a five-star hotel, it should meet the five-star standard, and details determine success or failure!
